];

let currentIndex = 0;
let sidebarVisible = false;
const player = document.getElementById('player');
const nowPlaying = document.getElementById('nowPlaying');
const videoList = document.getElementById('videoList');
const sidebar = document.getElementById('sidebar');
const menuTrigger = document.getElementById('menuTrigger');

// 生成列表
videos.forEach((video, index) => {
const li = document.createElement('li');
li.className = 'video-item' + (index === 0 ? ' active' : '');
li.innerHTML = `<span class="number">${String(index + 1).padStart(2, '0')}</span>${video.name}`;
li.onclick = () => playVideo(index);
videoList.appendChild(li);
});

function playVideo(index) {
currentIndex = index;
player.src = videos[index].url;
nowPlaying.textContent = `正在播放: ${videos[index].name}`;
player.play();
// 更新列表高亮
document.querySelectorAll('.video-item').forEach((item, i) => {
item.classList.toggle('active', i === index);
});
// 滚动到可见区域
document.querySelectorAll('.video-item')[index].scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'nearest' });
// 播放时隐藏侧边栏
sidebar.classList.remove('show');
sidebarVisible = false;
}

function prevVideo() {
playVideo(currentIndex > 0 ? currentIndex - 1 : videos.length - 1);
}

function nextVideo() {
playVideo(currentIndex < videos.length - 1 ? currentIndex + 1 : 0);
}

function toggleSidebar() {
sidebarVisible = !sidebarVisible;
sidebar.classList.toggle('show', sidebarVisible);
}

// 键盘快捷键
document.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
if (e.key === 'ArrowLeft' || e.key === 'ArrowUp') prevVideo();
if (e.key === 'ArrowRight' || e.key === 'ArrowDown') nextVideo();
if (e.key === 'Escape') {
sidebarVisible = false;
sidebar.classList.remove('show');
}
});
</script>
</body>
</html>
